<Rate>5</Rate>< Review>
Holy Heaven this place was great! I come from Washington state where we have some of the best sushi. Had only room for two rolls but they were fantastic!

Pros:The PJ roll was incredible, good creamy texture from the cream cheese, very decent flavor. My most favorite of the two: The Banana roll: Shrimp Tempura, cream cheese rolled topped with tempura banana and eel sauce (Though I recommend having the sauce on the side like I did, it was good but depending on your taste it may or may not go well with the banana.) Overall impressed with the service, very quick response and friendly!

The dessert I had was YUMMY, fried banana ice cream. Though I recommend staying off the whipped cream. The portion however was decent for two people.

Cons: Careful if you like sucking down coke or iced tea, no free refills, .95/glass, so savor it.

Stars: 4.5 out of 5

Highly recommend this place for those who love sushi.< /Review>

<Review>We have recently moved to the neighborhood and decided to go check out Sociale a few days ago. The ambiance is very charming and romantic, and I love it that the restaurant doesn't face the street. The area is nice and quiet. I have tons of food allergies and it's very challenging for me to eat at an Italian restaurant, considering that I am allergic to dairy, gluten, garlic and onions. We told the waitress about my allergies once we sat down and she couldn't be any more accommodating. She spoke with the chef and he/she put a seafood pasta dish together without all the allergens and it was absolutely DELICIOUS!! How can you make Italian food taste good without garlic I don't know lol. I hadn't had a pasta dish in years and it absolutely made my day. <Rating>5<//Rating>< Review>
My husband and I went to Sociale on a Friday night to celebrate our anniversary. We made reservations for 6pm, and we arrived about ten minutes early. We were immediately seated and offered water. We chose a half bottle of red (a very good Brunello) to have with dinner and let our server, Molly, know that one of us was a vegetarian. Molly was terrific throughout the entire meal, even wishing us a happy anniversary (which I had put on the reservation but neither of us had mentioned upon arrival). When I asked her preference between two entr√©es, she didn't hesitate to offer her opinion, which was really nice in contrast to places where you wonder if the people working there have ever sampled the menu. We enjoyed small but very yummy bread rolls while we waited for dinner.

We had a stone fruit and kale salad to start, followed by the wagu beef (for my husband) and the corn tortellini (for me) and polenta fries (to share). Everything was cooked very well and tasted delicious, and the portions were perfect.

For dessert, we enjoyed the orange flan and a vanilla milkshake with a fried dough pastry. Both were just as tasty as everything else we had shared and a perfect end to our meal. Dinner for the two of us, including a shared appetizer, two entrees, a shared side, two desserts, and a half bottle of wine came to about $180, which was very reasonable considering the terrific service and the delicious food. We'll definitely return!<//Review>

< Rating>
3</Rating>
<Review>Sociale is super cute. I love how it's hidden off the street between buildings. The main room and secondary room aesthetic seemed a bit off... a bit funeral home-y with the thick draperies over fake, brick walls and simple, white paint on other walls. Not a ton of charm on the interior, but the patio was adorable.

Service was spectacular - there was quite a long wait between starter and entree (the server didn't even take our dinner order until after the small plates were finished), as other reviewers had mentioned, but that didn't bother me so much. It was a very casual and relaxed environment to enjoy conversation and good food.

We had the fried olives and the pork belly, which were both delicious. They also serve small, warm biscuits/rolls with butter. I love that they were warm and... well... I love bread.

For dinner, I had the Wagyu Bavette Steak. I was a little disappointed - for the price, I really expected something pretty great, but it was a tough cut of meat that was overdone and had a pretty bland and overall game-y flavor.

The wine selection is pretty good and pretty extensive.

I would consider giving it another go and possibly trying the pasta instead, but at this point, I would not recommend to my friends.<//Review>< Pics>
None< /Pics>

< text>
Have been here twice in the last month. The place is pretty cheap. No touch carwash. Main complaint was with the way the car wash options are in the touch screen menu where you pay - it's designed to make you choose the most expensive one by default (I think it's at the top of the list). There is no back button to quickly change the selection too ü§∑üèΩ‚Äç‚ôÇÔ∏è.

The entire wash is automated - there is one person at the entrance who checks to make sure your wheels go into the rails properly. But because of the touch-less wash, sometimes your car comes out not very clean. Like, last time we had to manually pick a bunch of stuff off of my car, after the wash.

Also, I think the place uses too much water for the wash. I hope they recycle the water somehow.<//text>

We ordered our "spirit" table from Earthlite. It did arrive quickly. As we set it up we noticed that the legs have to be extended carefully as there is no support (unlike a much cheaper table we have)connecting the two legs from either end with each other, thus there is a risk of breaking part of the table if you do not hold both legs, one in each hand and move them simultaneously. As soon as we set it up and tested it out, one of the bed supports snapped. We called Earhtlite and left a message to which we never got a response. I called back and talked to someone who said it would be forwarded on and I should expect a call back. We did not get a return call so I called again. I explained my dilemma and this time they forwarded me on to one of their associates. I explained the situation and how we had clients booked expecting to have this additional table. Earthlite seemed indifferent to my plight and the fact that we had to call and move clients. We had to wait five days to get a replacement despite them being 5 hours away.
The Sierra Comfort table we had first is not as wide but seems just as sturdy and comfortable yet cost 1/5th the price.<//Text>

I'm disappointed. The elastic band of the new massage chair replacement cover is quite snug and when the seat cover is placed over the seat, it looks absolutely perfect - just like in the picture. BUT, when you sit on it and work on your client/patient and get up again, the back side has pulled up a bit and the seat cover gets wrinkly and looks dumb and messy. I've pulled it back many times now, and even tried overcompensating for the sliding by really making it as tight as possible in the back, but it creeps creeping up and looks stupid. I might bring in some thread and try tightening the bottom band more if possible (it might tear?). Or maybe I'll try stapling it on with a powerful stapler. <Rating>5<//Rating><text>I purchased my first table from you about twenty years ago. It was in perfect condition when I sold after fifteen years prior to my world traveling adventures. Now settled down again with a new set of clients, of course my choice was EarthLite.

Being pretty disappointed in, yet understanding of, the disguise of free shipping, I'll advise this company to make more bold the fine print that speaks of exclusions to that coupon.

An even greater disappointment was the promise of a three-business-day delivery. This important lesson taught me to wait to schedule clients until products arrive! Over the course of the next eight days, my trips to the post office twenty minutes away only led to further disgust because of the seemingly missing table. Low and behold, a voicemail finally comes from Fed-Ex stating the package had been there for about a week. How was I to know Fed-Ex didn't deliver to post offices? I wish I knew that piece of apparently common knowledge. This information needed to be posted in bold font when purchasing on-line!

And now for the great news...EarthLite agreed! They refunded the expensive shipping costs, and they even said 'thank you' for bringing this to their attention. Each of the customer service department members I had the pleasure of politely whining to was kind, patient, and willing to listen and take action.
Good going, EarthLite!< /text><pics>None< /pics>< Resp>
